    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      矩阵相加
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     两个形状相同的矩阵相加是指对应位置的元素相加：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         A 
        
       
         + 
        
       
         B 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol C=\boldsymbol A+\boldsymbol B
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7694em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            B
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          A 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         + 
        
        
        
          B 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
      
        C_{i,j}=A_{i,j}+B_{i,j}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
           C
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0715em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
           B
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0502em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      矩阵和标量
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     标量和矩阵相乘或相加时，矩阵的每个元素都和标量相乘或相加：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        D 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         a 
        
       
         ⋅ 
        
       
         B 
        
       
         + 
        
       
         c 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol D=a\cdot\boldsymbol B+c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0319em;">
            D
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          a
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ⋅
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7694em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            B
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        D 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         a 
        
       
         ⋅ 
        
        
        
          B 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         + 
        
       
         c 
        
       
      
        D_{i,j}=a\cdot B_{i,j}+c
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
           D
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0278em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4445em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          a
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ⋅
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
           B
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0502em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          c
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      矩阵和向量
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     深度学习允许矩阵与向量相加，此时向量和矩阵的每一列相加：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         A 
        
       
         + 
        
       
         b 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol C=\boldsymbol A+\boldsymbol b
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7694em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            b
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          A 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         + 
        
        
        
          b 
         
        
          j 
         
        
       
      
        C_{i,j}=A_{i,j}+b_j
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
           C
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0715em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9805em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           b
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                 j
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     这种隐式地复制向量到很多位置的方式称为
     <strong>
      广播
     </strong>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     <strong>
      矩阵相乘
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        m 
        
       
         × 
        
       
         n 
        
       
      
        m\times n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          m
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ×
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     与
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
         × 
        
       
         p 
        
       
      
        n\times p
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ×
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          p
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        B 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol B
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            B
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的矩阵乘积为
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        m 
        
       
         × 
        
       
         p 
        
       
      
        m\times p
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          m
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ×
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          p
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol C
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
        
       
         = 
        
        
         
         
           A 
          
         
           B 
          
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol C=\boldsymbol{AB}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            AB
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
         
         
           ∑ 
          
         
           k 
          
         
         
         
           A 
          
          
          
            i 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            k 
           
          
         
         
         
           B 
          
          
          
            k 
           
          
            , 
           
          
            j 
           
          
         
        
       
      
        C_{i,j}=\displaystyle\sum_kA_{i,k}B_{k,j}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
           C
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0715em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 2.3521em; vertical-align: -1.3021em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mop op-limits">
          <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
           <span class="vlist-r">
            <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.05em;">
             <span class="" style="top: -1.8479em; margin-left: 0em;">
              <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;">
              </span>
              <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
               <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">
                k
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="" style="top: -3.05em;">
              <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3.05em;">
              </span>
              <span class="">
               <span class="mop op-symbol large-op">
                ∑
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-s">
             ​
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="vlist-r">
            <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.3021em;">
             <span class="">
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">
                  k
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
           B
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0502em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">
                  k
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">
                  ,
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">
                  j
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2861em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     两个维数相同的向量
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol x
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            x
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     和
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        y 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol y
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6389em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.037em;">
            y
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的
     <strong>
      点积
     </strong>
     可看作矩阵乘积
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          ⊤ 
         
        
       
         y 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol x^\top\boldsymbol y
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0435em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol">
             x
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8491em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 ⊤
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.037em;">
            y
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     。
    </p>
    <p>
     矩阵乘积服从分配律和结合律，不服从交换律：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
         ( 
        
       
         B 
        
       
         + 
        
       
         C 
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
        
         
         
           A 
          
         
           B 
          
         
        
       
         + 
        
        
         
         
           A 
          
         
           C 
          
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A(\boldsymbol B+\boldsymbol C)=\boldsymbol{AB}+\boldsymbol{AC}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            B
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7694em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            AB
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          +
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            AC
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
         
         
           B 
          
         
           C 
          
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         ( 
        
        
         
         
           A 
          
         
           B 
          
         
        
       
         ) 
        
       
         C 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A(\boldsymbol{BC})=(\boldsymbol{AB})\boldsymbol C
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            BC
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mopen">
          (
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            AB
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mclose">
          )
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     向量点积服从交换律：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
        
          ⊤ 
         
        
       
         y 
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          y 
         
        
          ⊤ 
         
        
       
         x 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol x^\top\boldsymbol y=\boldsymbol y^\top\boldsymbol x
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0435em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol">
             x
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8491em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 ⊤
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.037em;">
            y
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0435em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.037em;">
             y
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8491em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 ⊤
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            x
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     两个形状相同的矩阵中对应位置的元素乘积称为
     <strong>
      元素对应乘积
     </strong>
     或者
     <strong>
      Hadamard乘积
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         A 
        
       
         ⊙ 
        
       
         B 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol C=\boldsymbol A\odot\boldsymbol B
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0698em;">
            C
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.7694em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mbin">
          ⊙
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0483em;">
            B
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        C 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          A 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
        
        
          B 
         
         
         
           i 
          
         
           , 
          
         
           j 
          
         
        
       
      
        C_{i,j}=A_{i,j}B_{i,j}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0715em;">
           C
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0715em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                  i
                 </span>
                 <span class="mpunct mtight">

                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0572em;">

             <span class="vlist-s">

              </span>

            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.9694em; vertical-align: -0.2861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           A
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">

           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">
           B
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3117em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0502em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">

    </p>
    <p>
     矩阵乘积可以表示
     <strong>
      线性方程组
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
          
         
           x 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         b 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol{Ax}=\boldsymbol b
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            Ax
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            b
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="_112">
     </a>
     单位矩阵和逆矩阵
    </h3>
    <p>
     <strong>
      单位矩阵
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        n 
        
       
      
        n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord mathnormal">
          n
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     阶
     <strong>
      单位矩阵
     </strong>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        I 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol I_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8361em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0778em;">
             I
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     沿主对角线的元素都是
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        1 
        
       
      
        1
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          1
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，其他元素都是
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        0 
        
       
      
        0
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          0
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        I 
         
        
          3 
         
        
       
         = 
        
        
         
         
           [ 
          
          
           
            
             
             
               1 
              
             
            
            
             
             
               0 
              
             
            
            
             
             
               0 
              
             
            
           
           
            
             
             
               0 
              
             
            
            
             
             
               1 
              
             
            
            
             
             
               0 
              
             
            
           
           
            
             
             
               0 
              
             
            
            
             
             
               0 
              
             
            
            
             
             
               1 
              
             
            
           
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol I_3=\displaystyle\begin{bmatrix}1&amp;0&amp;0\\0&amp;1&amp;0\\0&amp;0&amp;1\end{bmatrix}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8361em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0778em;">
             I
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 3
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">
              ​
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">
              <span class="">
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 3.6em; vertical-align: -1.55em;">
         </span>

                <span class="" style="top: -3.01em;">

    <p>
     任何向量和单位矩阵相乘都不变：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        ∀ 
        
       
         x 
        
       
         ∈ 
        
        
        
          R 
         
        
          n

          I 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
         x 
        
       
         = 
        
       
         x 
        
       
      
        \forall\boldsymbol x\in\mathbb R^n,\boldsymbol I_n\boldsymbol x=\boldsymbol x

       <span class="katex-html">

    <p>
     <strong>
      逆矩阵
     </strong>
    </p>
    <p>
     矩阵
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     的
     <strong>
      逆矩阵
     </strong>
     记作
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
         
         
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A^{-1}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8901em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol">
             A
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8901em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.139em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1

            </span>

          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
     ，满足如下条件：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
         
         
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         A 
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          I 
         
        
          n 
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A^{-1}\boldsymbol A=\boldsymbol I_n
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8901em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol">
             A
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8901em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.139em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  −
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8361em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0778em;">
             I
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                 n
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
             <span class="vlist-s">

    <p>
     也可以定义逆矩阵右乘：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A

           − 
          
         
           1

          n 
         
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol A\boldsymbol A^{-1}=\boldsymbol I_n

         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            A
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord boldsymbol">
             A
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>

                <span class="mord mtight">

                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>

             </span>
            </span>
           </span>

         </span>

          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.8361em; vertical-align: -0.15em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">

            <span class="mord boldsymbol" style="margin-right: 0.0778em;">
             I
            </span>
           </span>

            <span class="vlist-r">

             </span>
            </span>

             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;">

              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>

    </p>
    <p>
     这两个逆矩阵分别为左逆和右逆，方阵的左逆和右逆相等。
    </p>
    <p>
     通过矩阵求逆可以求解上述线性方程组：
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        A 
          
         
           x 
          
         
        
       
         = 
        
       
         b 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol{Ax}=\boldsymbol b
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6861em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            Ax
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mrel">
          =
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
         </span>
        </span>
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            b
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </span>
     </span>
    </p>
    <p>
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
        
       
         = 
        
        
        
          A 
         
         
         
           − 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
       
         b 
        
       
      
        \boldsymbol x=\boldsymbol A^{-1}\boldsymbol b
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4444em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord">
           <span class="mord boldsymbol">
            x
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">

               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
